{"id":"567666a1-a274-4ac9-baa4-836d57b85a7c","timestamp":"2025-08-29T12:30:25.686Z","instructions":"# AGENTS.md - Lightship Fund Analysis App\r\n\r\n## Project Overview\r\nEnterprise-grade fund analysis platform for Raymond James wealth management advisors. Features sophisticated server-side scoring algorithms, real-time data ingestion, comprehensive reporting, and investment committee-ready visualizations.\r\n\r\n## Current Architecture\r\n- **Frontend**: React 19 with TypeScript, functional components and hooks\r\n- **Backend**: Supabase (PostgreSQL) with custom RPCs and materialized views\r\n- **Hosting**: Vercel with serverless functions\r\n- **Scoring Engine**: Z-score based ranking with configurable profiles and weights\r\n- **Data Pipeline**: CSV ingestion with EOM normalization and validation\r\n- **Export**: Professional PDF reports via React-PDF, Excel/CSV exports\r\n\r\n## Development Philosophy\r\n- **Accuracy First**: This impacts real investment decisions - calculations must be mathematically precise\r\n- **Server-Side Performance**: Heavy computations in PostgreSQL, not client browser\r\n- **Advisor-Centric**: Optimized for monthly investment committee workflows\r\n- **Explainable AI**: Scoring model must be transparent and client-presentable\r\n- **Enterprise Ready**: Audit trails, data governance, and compliance-ready\r\n\r\n## Key Features to Understand\r\n\r\n### 1. **Sophisticated Scoring System**\r\n- **Server-side computation**: Scoring runs in PostgreSQL via RPCs for consistency\r\n- **Multiple scoring models**: Different algorithms for equity vs fixed income vs alternatives\r\n- **Z-score methodology**: Statistical ranking within asset class peer groups\r\n- **Configurable weights**: Admin can adjust metric importance per asset class\r\n- **Breakdown transparency**: Each score shows per-metric contributions\r\n\r\n### 2. **Data Architecture**\r\n- **Monthly snapshots**: End-of-month (EOM) normalized performance data\r\n- **Asset class resolution**: Sophisticated mapping with primary benchmark assignment\r\n- **Audit trails**: All changes tracked with user attribution and timestamps\r\n- **Research notes**: Append-only decision logs per fund with decision context\r\n\r\n### 3. **Professional Reporting**\r\n- **Investment committee PDFs**: Multi-table layouts with Apple-quality design\r\n- **Excel exports**: Formatted for financial analysis with consistent number formatting\r\n- **Interactive dashboards**: Real-time data with drill-down capabilities\r\n\r\n## Core Business Logic\r\n\r\n### Scoring Algorithm (src/services/scoring.js)\r\n```javascript\r\n// Z-score based ranking within asset class peer groups\r\n// Excludes benchmarks from peer statistics\r\n// Configurable weights via scoring profiles\r\n// Returns 0-100 scale with breakdown details\r\n\r\nfinal_score = Î£(weight_i Ã— z_score_i) * normalization_factor\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Data Flow Architecture\r\n```\r\nCSV Upload â†’ Validation â†’ EOM Conversion â†’ Supabase â†’ RPC Processing â†’ \r\nâ†’ Materialized Views â†’ React Components â†’ Professional Exports\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Asset Class & Benchmark Resolution\r\n- **Primary benchmarks**: Each asset class mapped to designated ETF\r\n- **Performance deltas**: Automatic calculation vs benchmark\r\n- **Missing data handling**: Graceful degradation with fallback values\r\n\r\n## Database Schema (Supabase)\r\n\r\n### Core Tables\r\n```sql\r\n-- Fund registry and performance\r\nfunds (id, ticker, name, asset_class_id, created_at)\r\nfund_performance (ticker, date, ytd_return, one_year_return, ..., expense_ratio)\r\nasset_classes (id, name, primary_benchmark_id)\r\nbenchmarks (id, ticker, name, asset_class_id)\r\nbenchmark_performance (ticker, date, ytd_return, ...)\r\n\r\n-- Scoring system\r\nscoring_profiles (id, name, is_default, created_at)\r\nscoring_weights (id, profile_id, scope, scope_id, metric, weight)\r\nmetric_stats_as_of (asset_class_id, date, metric, mean, stddev, count)\r\nscores_as_of (asset_class_id, fund_ticker, date, score_final, breakdown)\r\n\r\n-- Governance and audit\r\nfund_research_notes (id, fund_id, note, decision, created_at, author)\r\nactivity_logs (id, user_id, action, details, created_at)\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Key RPCs (Performance Critical)\r\n```sql\r\n-- Data retrieval\r\nget_funds_as_of(p_date) â†’ enriched fund data with performance\r\nget_asset_class_table(p_date, p_asset_class_id, p_include_benchmark) â†’ scored funds + benchmark\r\nget_scores_as_of(p_date, p_asset_class_id, p_limit, p_after) â†’ paginated scored results\r\nget_compare_dataset(p_date, p_tickers[]) â†’ side-by-side comparison data\r\n\r\n-- Scoring computation\r\nrefresh_metric_stats_as_of(p_date) â†’ compute peer group statistics\r\nrefresh_scores_as_of(p_date) â†’ compute all fund scores for date\r\n```\r\n\r\n## Code Guidelines\r\n\r\n### When Adding Features\r\n- **Check existing patterns**: Leverage established services and components\r\n- **Server-side first**: Move computations to PostgreSQL when possible\r\n- **Maintain scoring accuracy**: Any changes to scoring logic require mathematical validation\r\n- **Feature flags**: Use environment variables for gradual rollouts\r\n- **Test with real data**: Raymond James production-like datasets\r\n\r\n### Component Development\r\n- **Composition over complexity**: Reuse existing dashboard components\r\n- **Performance conscious**: Virtualize large fund lists, debounce searches\r\n- **Professional styling**: Raymond James brand standards with Apple-quality polish\r\n- **Accessibility**: Proper ARIA labels and keyboard navigation\r\n- **Error boundaries**: Graceful failure handling for advisor workflows\r\n\r\n### Data Processing Standards\r\n```javascript\r\n// Preferred patterns\r\nconst fundsByAssetClass = funds.filter(f => f.asset_class_id === targetId);\r\nconst cleanTicker = ticker?.toUpperCase().trim().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]/g, '');\r\nconst safeNumber = value => isNaN(value) ? null : parseFloat(value);\r\n\r\n// Use centralized formatting\r\nimport { fmt } from '../utils/fmt';\r\nconst displayPercent = fmt.percent(value, { decimals: 2, sign: true });\r\n```\r\n\r\n## Current Tech Stack\r\n\r\n### Frontend\r\n- **React 19** with functional components and hooks\r\n- **TypeScript** for type safety and better developer experience\r\n- **Tailwind CSS** for consistent styling and rapid development\r\n- **Lucide React** for professional iconography\r\n- **React-PDF** for investment committee report generation\r\n\r\n### Backend & Data\r\n- **Supabase** (PostgreSQL) with Row Level Security\r\n- **Custom SQL functions** for complex business logic\r\n- **Materialized views** for performance optimization\r\n- **JSONB storage** for flexible metadata and audit trails\r\n\r\n### Development & Deployment\r\n- **Vercel** for hosting with serverless functions\r\n- **Environment-based feature flags** for safe deployments\r\n- **Comprehensive testing** with Jest and React Testing Library\r\n- **Performance monitoring** with custom benchmarking harness\r\n\r\n## Performance Targets\r\n\r\n### Database Operations (95th percentile)\r\n- `get_funds_as_of`: < 800ms\r\n- `get_asset_class_table`: < 1200ms  \r\n- `refresh_scores_as_of`: < 5000ms\r\n- CSV import (500 rows): < 10000ms\r\n\r\n### UI Responsiveness\r\n- Dashboard load: < 3 seconds\r\n- Table sorting/filtering: < 500ms\r\n- PDF generation: < 30 seconds\r\n- Export operations: < 15 seconds\r\n\r\n## Security & Compliance\r\n\r\n### Data Protection\r\n- **Fund data confidentiality**: No external API calls with sensitive data\r\n- **Audit trails**: Complete change tracking for compliance\r\n- **Input validation**: Comprehensive sanitization of all user inputs\r\n- **Role-based access**: Ready for multi-advisor deployment\r\n\r\n### Development Security\r\n- **Environment variable protection**: No secrets in client code\r\n- **SQL injection prevention**: Parameterized queries and RPC patterns\r\n- **XSS protection**: Input sanitization and output encoding\r\n- **CSRF protection**: Supabase built-in security measures\r\n\r\n## Testing Priorities\r\n\r\n### Mathematical Accuracy\r\n- **Scoring calculations**: Z-score computations and weight applications\r\n- **Statistical functions**: Mean, standard deviation, percentile calculations\r\n- **Performance attribution**: Delta calculations vs benchmarks\r\n- **Export consistency**: Identical data across PDF/Excel/CSV formats\r\n\r\n### Data Integrity\r\n- **EOM conversion**: Date normalization accuracy\r\n- **Asset class mapping**: Fund categorization correctness  \r\n- **Benchmark resolution**: Primary benchmark assignment logic\r\n- **Historical data**: Snapshot consistency over time\r\n\r\n### User Workflows\r\n- **Admin panel operations**: CRUD operations Please review the current implementation to understand the architecture, data models, and user workflows.\r\nCurrent State Production fund analytics app serving 4 advisors with:\r\n* Dashboard showing ~149 funds with performance data\r\n* Asset class analysis across 32 categories\r\n* PDF report generation\r\n* Admin data management\r\n* Monthly performance data imports (manual CSV process)\r\nAvailable Expansion Data Sources I have access to additional Raymond James data that could enhance the app:\r\n1. $$\\r\\n  WITH cand AS (\\r\\n    SELECT COALESCE(\\r\\n      (SELECT MAX(date) FROM public.fund_performance WHERE date <= COALESCE(p_hint, public._get_latest_fund_date())),\\r\\n      (SELECT Iâ€™ll proceed with percent-based expense ratios (0.94 = 0.94%) and include cash grouped with money markets.\n\nHereâ€™s a focused, ready-to-implement package: migrations, import specs, and API endpoints that fit your current stack (Supabase + Vercel serverless + React).\n\n**What Iâ€™ll Add**\n- SQL migration: holdings/trades tables, ingest_files, two materialized views, three RPCs.\n- Serverless import endpoints: normalize + hash + (optionally) upsert.\n- Parsing utilities: robust currency/date/ticker parsing + deterministic hashing.\n- Minimal UI note: add â€œAsâ€‘of Monthâ€ to holdings upload (same pattern as performance).\n\n**SQL Migration**\n- Path: `supabase/migrations/20250829_holdings_trades.sql`\n- Creates tables, indexes, mat views, and RPCs (idempotent). Grants match current pattern.\n\n```sql\n-- Holdings & Trades Core (idempotent)\ncreate extension if not exists pgcrypto;\n\n-- Ingest file manifest\ncreate table if not exists public.ingest_files (\n  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),\n  source text not null check (source in ('holdings','trades')),\n  file_name text not null,\n  period_month date,\n  row_count integer,\n  checksum text,\n  processed_at timestamptz,\n  status text not null default 'processed' check (status in ('pending','processed','failed')),\n  error text\n);\n\n-- Holdings snapshots\ncreate table if not exists public.holdings_snapshots (\n  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),\n  as_of_date date not null,\n  advisor_id text not null,\n  account_id_hash text not null,\n  ticker text null,\n  cusip text null,\n  quantity numeric not null,\n  market_value numeric not null,\n  price numeric null,\n  cost_basis_per_share numeric null,\n  unrealized_gain_loss_total numeric null,\n  asset_category_label text null,\n  first_acq_date date null,\n  expense_ratio_net numeric null, -- e.g., 0.94 means 0.94%\n  share_class text null,\n  account_type text null,\n  registration_type text null,\n  product_name text null,\n  product_subtype text null,\n  product_type text null,\n  source_file_id uuid null references public.ingest_files(id) on delete set null,\n  raw_row_hash text null,\n  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),\n  constraint holdings_unique_row unique (as_of_date, advisor_id, account_id_hash, coalesce(cusip, ticker))\n);\ncreate index if not exists idx_holdings_asof_advisor on public.holdings_snapshots (as_of_date, advisor_id);\ncreate index if not exists idx_holdings_security on public.holdings_snapshots (coalesce(cusip, ticker));\n\n-- Trades\ncreate table if not exists public.trades (\n  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),\n  trade_date date not null,\n  settle_date date null,\n  advisor_id text not null,\n  account_id_hash text not null,\n  branch_code text null,\n  side text not null check (side in ('BUY','SELL')),\n  product_type text null,\n  money_position_type text null,\n  ticker text null,\n  cusip text null,\n  quantity numeric not null,\n  price numeric null,\n  principal_amount numeric not null,  -- always positive; sign implied by side\n  amount_signed numeric null,         -- optional raw sign amount\n  trade_id text null,\n  product_description text null,\n  cancelled_flag boolean null,\n  discretionary_trade boolean null,\n  time_price_discretion boolean null,\n  source_file_id uuid null references public.ingest_files(id) on delete set null,\n  raw_row_hash text null,\n  created_at timestamptz not null default now()\n);\ncreate index if not exists idx_trades_date on public.trades (trade_date);\ncreate index if not exists idx_trades_advisor_date on public.trades (advisor_id, trade_date);\ncreate index if not exists idx_trades_security_date on public.trades (coalesce(cusip, ticker), trade_date);\n\n-- Mat view: holdings aggregation (advisor-level)\ncreate materialized view if not exists public.holdings_agg_as_of as\nwith base as (\n  select\n    as_of_date,\n    advisor_id,\n    coalesce(cusip, ticker) as security_key,\n    ticker,\n    cusip,\n    product_type,\n    sum(market_value) as total_value,\n    sum(quantity) as total_qty,\n    count(distinct account_id_hash) as accounts_count\n  from public.holdings_snapshots\n  group by 1,2,3,4,5,6\n), totals as (\n  select as_of_date, advisor_id, sum(total_value) as advisor_total_value\n  from base group by 1,2\n)\nselect\n  b.as_of_date,\n  b.advisor_id,\n  b.security_key,\n  b.ticker,\n  b.cusip,\n  case\n    when (b.ticker is null and b.cusip is null) then 'CASH_EQUIVALENT'\n    when b.product_type ilike '%Cash%' then 'CASH_EQUIVALENT'\n    when b.product_type ilike '%Money Market%' then 'CASH_EQUIVALENT'\n    else 'SECURITY'\n  end as class,\n  b.total_value,\n  b.total_qty,\n  b.accounts_count,\n  (b.total_value / nullif(t.advisor_total_value,0))::numeric as percent_of_advisor_portfolio\nfrom base b\njoin totals t\n  on t.as_of_date = b.as_of_date and t.advisor_id = b.advisor_id;\ncreate index if not exists idx_holdings_agg_asof on public.holdings_agg_as_of (as_of_date, advisor_id);\n\n-- Mat view: fund flows (monthly)\ncreate materialized view if not exists public.fund_flows_as_of as\nselect\n  date_trunc('month', trade_date)::date as month,\n  advisor_id,\n  coalesce(cusip, ticker) as security_key,\n  ticker,\n  cusip,\n  sum(case when side='BUY' then principal_amount else 0 end) as inflows,\n  sum(case when side='SELL' then principal_amount else 0 end) as outflows,\n  (sum(case when side='BUY' then principal_amount else 0 end)\n   - sum(case when side='SELL' then principal_amount else 0 end)) as net_flow,\n  count(distinct advisor_id) as advisors_trading\nfrom public.trades\nwhere cancelled_flag is distinct from true\ngroup by 1,2,3,4,5;\ncreate index if not exists idx_fund_flows_month on public.fund_flows_as_of (month, advisor_id);\n\n-- RPC: refresh mat views\ncreate or replace function public.refresh_holdings_agg_as_of()\nreturns void language sql as $$ refresh materialized view concurrently public.holdings_agg_as_of; $$;\ncreate or replace function public.refresh_fund_flows_as_of()\nreturns void language sql as $$ refresh materialized view concurrently public.fund_flows_as_of; $$;\ngrant execute on function public.refresh_holdings_agg_as_of() to anon, authenticated, service_role;\ngrant execute on function public.refresh_fund_flows_as_of() to anon, authenticated, service_role;\n\n-- RPC: holdings agg retrieval\ncreate or replace function public.get_holdings_agg_as_of(\n  p_date date, p_advisor_id text default null, p_limit int default 100, p_offset int default 0\n)\nreturns setof public.holdings_agg_as_of\nlanguage sql stable as $$\n  select * from public.holdings_agg_as_of\n  where (p_date is null or as_of_date = p_date)\n    and (p_advisor_id is null or advisor_id = p_advisor_id)\n  order by total_value desc nulls last\n  limit p_limit offset p_offset;\n$$;\ngrant execute on function public.get_holdings_agg_as_of(date, text, int, int) to anon, authenticated, service_role;\n\n-- RPC: flows retrieval\ncreate or replace function public.get_fund_flows(\n  p_start date, p_end date, p_advisor_id text default null, p_security_key text default null\n)\nreturns table (\n  month date, advisor_id text, security_key text, ticker text, cusip text,\n  inflows numeric, outflows numeric, net_flow numeric\n)\nlanguage sql stable as $$\n  select month, advisor_id, security_key, ticker, cusip, inflows, outflows, net_flow\n  from public.fund_flows_as_of\n  where (p_start is null or month >= date_trunc('month', p_start))\n    and (p_end is null or month <= date_trunc('month', p_end))\n    and (p_advisor_id is null or advisor_id = p_advisor_id)\n    and (p_security_key is null or security_key = p_security_key)\n  order by month desc, net_flow desc nulls last;\n$$;\ngrant execute on function public.get_fund_flows(date, date, text, text) to anon, authenticated, service_role;\n```\n\n**Serverless Endpoints**\n- Paths:\n  - `api/import/holdings.js`: accepts JSON `{ asOfDate, csvText, fileName }`\n  - `api/import/trades.js`: accepts JSON `{ csvText, fileName }`\n- Behavior:\n  - Parse CSV, normalize fields, hash account IDs using server-only `HOLDINGS_CLIENT_ID_SALT`.\n  - Compute `raw_row_hash` for idempotency.\n  - If `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` is set, upsert directly; otherwise return normalized rows and client can upsert using existing supabase client (if grants permit).\n\nParsing utilities (shared):\n- Path: `src/server/ingest/utils.js`\n\n```js\n// src/server/ingest/utils.js\nimport crypto from 'crypto';\n\nexport const currencyToNumber = (s) => {\n  if (s == null) return null;\n  const str = String(s).replace(/\\$/g, '').replace(/,/g, '').trim();\n  if (!str) return null;\n  const neg = /^\\(.*\\)$/.test(str);\n  const val = parseFloat(str.replace(/[()]/g, ''));\n  if (Number.isNaN(val)) return null;\n  return neg ? -val : val;\n};\n\nexport const parseYN = (s) => {\n  const v = String(s || '').trim().toUpperCase();\n  return v === 'Y' ? true : v === 'N' ? false : null;\n};\n\nexport const parseDateMDY = (s) => {\n  if (!s) return null;\n  const d = new Date(s);\n  return Number.isNaN(d.getTime()) ? null : new Date(Date.UTC(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), d.getDate())).toISOString().slice(0,10);\n};\n\nexport const normalizeTicker = (s) => {\n  const t = String(s || '').toUpperCase().trim();\n  return t || null;\n};\n\nexport const hashAccountId = (accountId) => {\n  const salt = process.env.HOLDINGS_CLIENT_ID_SALT || '';\n  if (!salt) throw new Error('HOLDINGS_CLIENT_ID_SALT is not configured');\n  return crypto.createHmac('sha256', salt).update(String(accountId || '').trim()).digest('hex');\n};\n\nexport const rowHash = (obj) => {\n  const sorted = Object.keys(obj).sort().reduce((acc,k)=>{ acc[k]=obj[k]; return acc; },{});\n  const json = JSON.stringify(sorted);\n  return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(json).digest('hex');\n};\n```\n\nHoldings endpoint (core mapping shown; upsert optional):\n\n```js\n// api/import/holdings.js\nimport { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';\nimport Papa from 'papaparse';\nimport { currencyToNumber, parseDateMDY, normalizeTicker, hashAccountId, rowHash } from '../../src/server/ingest/utils.js';\n\nexport default async function handler(req, res) {\n  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');\n  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'POST, OPTIONS');\n  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');\n  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();\n  if (req.method !== 'POST') return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Method not allowed' });\n\n  const { asOfDate, csvText, fileName } = req.body || {};\n  if (!asOfDate || !csvText) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'asOfDate and csvText are required' });\n\n  try {\n    const { data: rows, errors } = Papa.parse(csvText, { header: true, skipEmptyLines: true });\n    if (errors?.length) console.warn('CSV parse warnings:', errors.slice(0,3));\n\n    const out = [];\n    for (const r of rows) {\n      const advisor_id = String(r['FA #'] || '').trim();\n      const account = String(r['Account #'] || '').trim();\n      const account_id_hash = hashAccountId(account);\n\n      const symbol = normalizeTicker(r['Symbol']);\n      const cusip = String(r['CUSIP'] || '').trim() || null;\n      const price = currencyToNumber(r['Price']);\n      const quantity = Number(String(r['Quantity'] || '0').replace(/,/g,'').trim() || 0);\n      const market_value = currencyToNumber(r['Current Value']);\n      const cbs = currencyToNumber(r['Avg Cost/Share']);\n      const ugl = currencyToNumber(r['Unrealized G/L']);\n\n      // Skip empty â€œsummaryâ€ rows\n      if (!symbol && !cusip && (market_value == null || market_value === 0)) continue;\n\n      const rec = {\n        as_of_date: asOfDate,\n        advisor_id,\n        account_id_hash,\n        ticker: symbol || (cusip ? null : null), // CASH will be classified downstream\n        cusip,\n        quantity,\n        market_value,\n        price,\n        cost_basis_per_share: cbs,\n        unrealized_gain_loss_total: ugl,\n        asset_category_label: r['M* Category'] || null,\n        first_acq_date: parseDateMDY(r['First Acq Date']),\n        expense_ratio_net: r['Net Exp Ratio'] != null ? Number(r['Net Exp Ratio']) : null, // 0.94 = 0.94%\n        share_class: r['Share Class'] || null,\n        account_type: r['Account Type'] || null,\n        registration_type: r['Registration Type'] || null,\n        product_name: r['Product Name'] || null,\n        product_subtype: r['Product Subtype'] || null,\n        product_type: r['Product Type'] || null\n      };\n      rec.raw_row_hash = rowHash({ ...rec, account_id_hash }); // no raw account stored\n      out.push(rec);\n    }\n\n    const supabaseUrl = process.env.REACT_APP_SUPABASE_URL || process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL;\n    const serviceKey = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY; // optional\n    if (supabaseUrl && serviceKey) {\n      const sb = createClient(supabaseUrl, serviceKey, { auth: { persistSession: false } });\n      const { data: fileRow } = await sb.from('ingest_files').insert({\n        source: 'holdings', file_name: fileName || 'holdings.csv', period_month: asOfDate, row_count: out.length, status: 'processed'\n      }).select('id').single();\n\n      const batch = out.map(r => ({ ...r, source_file_id: fileRow?.id || null }));\n      // Upsert on unique key\n      const { error } = await sb.from('holdings_snapshots').upsert(batch, {\n        onConflict: 'as_of_date,advisor_id,account_id_hash,cusip,ticker' // coalesce handled via unique constraint\n      });\n      if (error) throw error;\n\n      await sb.rpc('refresh_holdings_agg_as_of');\n      return res.status(200).json({ inserted: out.length, mode: 'server-upsert' });\n    }\n\n    return res.status(200).json({ normalized: out.length, rows: out.slice(0, 5000), mode: 'normalize-only' });\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.error('Holdings import failed:', e);\n    return res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });\n  }\n}\n```\n\nTrades endpoint (highlights and mapping from your CSV):\n\n```js\n// api/import/trades.js\nimport { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';\nimport Papa from 'papaparse';\nimport { currencyToNumber, parseDateMDY, normalizeTicker, hashAccountId, rowHash, parseYN } from '../../src/server/ingest/utils.js';\n\nconst toSide = (s) => {\n  const v = String(s || '').toLowerCase();\n  return v.includes('purchase') || v === 'buy' ? 'BUY'\n       : v.includes('sale') || v === 'sell' ? 'SELL' : null;\n};\n\nexport default async function handler(req, res) {\n  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');\n  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'POST, OPTIONS');\n  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');\n  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') return res.status(200).end();\n  if (req.method !== 'POST') return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Method not allowed' });\n\n  const { csvText, fileName } = req.body || {};\n  if (!csvText) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'csvText is required' });\n\n  try {\n    const { data: rows, errors } = Papa.parse(csvText, { header: true, skipEmptyLines: true });\n    if (errors?.length) console.warn('CSV parse warnings:', errors.slice(0,3));\n\n    const out = [];\n    for (const r of rows) {\n      const advisor_id = String(r['FA'] || '').trim();\n      const account = String(r['Account'] || '').trim();\n      const account_id_hash = hashAccountId(account);\n\n      const side = toSide(r['Transaction Type']);\n      if (!side) continue;\n\n      const sharesRaw = String(r['Shares'] || '').replace(/,/g,'').trim();\n      const amount = currencyToNumber(r['Amount']);\n      const price = Number(String(r['Price'] || '').trim() || 0);\n      const qty = Math.abs(Number(sharesRaw || 0)); // absolute; side carries the sign\n      if (!qty && !amount) continue;\n\n      const rec = {\n        trade_date: parseDateMDY(r['Trade Date']),\n        settle_date: parseDateMDY(r['Settlement Date']),\n        advisor_id,\n        account_id_hash,\n        branch_code: String(r['Branch'] || '').trim() || null,\n        side,\n        product_type: r['Product Type'] || null,\n        money_position_type: r['Money Position Type'] || null,\n        ticker: normalizeTicker(r['Symbol']),\n        cusip: String(r['CUSIP'] || '').trim() || null,\n        quantity: qty,\n        price: Number.isFinite(price) ? price : null,\n        principal_amount: Math.abs(Number(amount || 0)),\n        amount_signed: Number(amount || 0),\n        trade_id: String(r['Trade Number'] || '').trim() || null,\n        product_description: r['Product Description'] || null,\n        cancelled_flag: parseYN(r['Cancelled Flag']),\n        discretionary_trade: parseYN(r['Discretionary Trade']),\n        time_price_discretion: parseYN(r['Time-Price Discretion'])\n      };\n      rec.raw_row_hash = rowHash({ ...rec, account_id_hash });\n      out.push(rec);\n    }\n\n    const supabaseUrl = process.env.REACT_APP_SUPABASE_URL || process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL;\n    const serviceKey = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;\n    if (supabaseUrl && serviceKey) {\n      const sb = createClient(supabaseUrl, serviceKey, { auth: { persistSession: false } });\n      const { data: fileRow } = await sb.from('ingest_files').insert({\n        source: 'trades', file_name: fileName || 'trades.csv',\n        period_month: out[0]?.trade_date?.slice(0,7) ? (out[0].trade_date.slice(0,7) + '-01') : null,\n        row_count: out.length, status: 'processed'\n      }).select('id').single();\n\n      const batch = out.map(r => ({ ...r, source_file_id: fileRow?.id || null }));\n      // De-dupe by row hash; rely on unique combos later if added\n      const { error } = await sb.from('trades').insert(batch);\n      if (error) throw error;\n\n      await sb.rpc('refresh_fund_flows_as_of');\n      return res.status(200).json({ inserted: out.length, mode: 'server-insert' });\n    }\n\n    return res.status(200).json({ normalized: out.length, rows: out.slice(0, 5000), mode: 'normalize-only' });\n  } catch (e) {\n    console.error('Trades import failed:', e);\n    return res.status(500).json({ error: e.message });\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Upload UI**\n- Holdings: add a required â€œAsâ€‘of Monthâ€ selector (same pattern as `MonthlySnapshotUpload.jsx`), and post `csvText` + `asOfDate` to `api/import/holdings`.\n- Trades: post `csvText` to `api/import/trades`; optionally restrict to selected month for QA.\n- Show server responses (inserted/normalized counts) and prompt to download error CSV if any.\n\n**Validation & Idempotency**\n- Holdings: upsert on `(as_of_date, advisor_id, account_id_hash, coalesce(cusip,ticker))` so re-uploads replace prior.\n- Trades: insert-only with `raw_row_hash` (dedupe by skipping duplicates client-side or add unique index over `raw_row_hash` later if desired).\n- Views: call refresh RPCs after imports.\n\n**Environment**\n- Add `HOLDINGS_CLIENT_ID_SALT` (server-only) in Vercel project settings.\n- Optional: add `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` (server-only) to let serverless write directly.\n- Do not expose either to the client (no `REACT_APP_` prefix).\n\n**Next Steps**\n- Approve me to add the files:\n  - `supabase/migrations/20250829_holdings_trades.sql`\n  - `src/server/ingest/utils.js`\n  - `api/import/holdings.js`\n  - `api/import/trades.js`\n- Then you can:\n  - Set `HOLDINGS_CLIENT_ID_SALT` in Vercel.\n  - (Optional) Set `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` to enable server-side upserts.\n  - Deploy and run the migration via your normal Supabase workflow.\n  - Upload your two CSVs via the new endpoints.\n\nWant me to apply the patch adding these files and wire them into your repo now?"}]}
